<H>{@sAraLA mahAbhArata@}

<H>{@bhISmapac bonGa@}

<H>{@gaNezaGka bandanA@}



<P>jay1atu dadhimaGgaLa jay1a bighnarAja

<P>drazane mukati ye prasanne karu siddha sac bonGakAryya | 1 |

<P>saMsiddha puruSa tu sac bonGadA rase bhoLa

<P>muhiM tote bheTili zwetagaGgara kULa | 2 |

<P>Adi abatAre zUdrika nAme brahmA

<P>aneka kALa ban~thAilI yebaNa mahAtamA | 3 |

<P>bharaharaSa nAyaka nRtyarase bheLA

<P>mahArase rasika nAtha tANDaba nRtyakaLA | 4 |

<P>sita pIta kuMkuma yAra zirare sitAMzu

<P>dinakara teja harai yAhAra zrIbhuje tIkhaparazu | 5 |

<P>yogAnanda puruSa tu bale mahAmeru

<P>tu yAku prasanna gata Agata tAku Sphuru | 6 |

<P>swAmI kArttaka prahAra ye kale bAma pAdaghAte

<P>daSi Na danta bhagnagalI anujara kopa catte | 7 |

<P>se bhagnadanta paDDalI upare pRthI se bhagnadantabhare | 8 |



[MBO-07-2]



<H1>{@mahAbharata@}



<P>yahuM se baDa Arata hoilI dharaNI

<P>basudhA rAsAiGgate tusti kale zULapANi | 9 |

<P>sacarAcara pRthrabIki Daddhara parzupANi

<P>bAma bhmaje saMharaNa nAtha kalu tAhA ANi | 10 |

<P>kope zApya tAku dilu ye turite

<P>galUta kuSThabyAdhna hoilA kArttikara | 11 |

<P>drodakarma kalI na galI tAku pAra

<P>rakta mAMse pUtta gaddha bahai rudhira | 12 |

<P>hara pAbonGatI boile doSa kalu y1amA

<P>tA kaSga dekhi day1Akala ye mahAtmA | 13 |

<P>kopa zAnti yeNu nuAriI tohora

<P>galUta kuSThabyAdhi hoilA kArtikara | 14 |

<P>ApAda zAnti kari ruhAilu kaya | 15 |

<P>abhay1e puruSa tu gajAnana mUrtta | 16 |

<P>calilIka medinI tohora pAdabhIra | 17 |

<P>aGga rakta barNNa sahiSNu ye meru

<P>brahmANDa mampai bAjante yAhAra Damwaru | 18 |

<H>{@ziba o biSNuGkara staba@}



<P>jay1a jayLa nAtha kAmenI mohana manasija

<P>bighaMsita kamala birAjai yAhAra pAda paMkaja | 1 |

<P>yoge yogezwara tu prasanne parama rUpa

<P>hele nibArilu krutAntaka darpa | 2 |

<P>paNTita janaMkara hrude tu kamala puSwamAli
